[[H271|Ahaz]] [[H6242|was twenty]] [[H1121|years old]] [[H4427|when he became king,]] [[H4427|and he reigned]] [[H3389|in Jerusalem]] [[H8337|sixteen]] [[H8141|years.]] [[H1732|And unlike David]] [[H1|his forefather,]] [[H3808|he did not]] [[H6213|do]] ⟨what was⟩ [[H3477|right]] [[H5869|in the eyes]] [[H3068|of the LORD.]] ^2801

[[H1980|Instead, he walked]] [[H1870|in the way]] [[H4428|of the kings]] [[H3478|of Israel]] [[H1571|and even]] [[H6213|made]] [[H4541|cast images]] [[H1168|of the Baals.]] ^2802

[[H1931|Moreover, Ahaz]] [[H6999|burned incense]] [[H1516|in the Valley of Hinnom]] [[H1197|and sacrificed]] [[H1121|his sons]] [[H784|in the fire,]] [[H8441|according to the abominations]] [[H1471|of the nations]] [[H834|whom]] [[H3423|the LORD]] [[H3068|had driven out]] [[H6440|before]] [[H1121|the Israelites.]] ^2803

[[H2076|And he sacrificed]] [[H6999|and burned incense]] [[H1116|on the high places,]] [[H5921|on]] [[H1389|the hills,]] [[H8478|and under]] [[H3605|every]] [[H7488|green]] [[H6086|tree.]] ^2804

[[H3068|So the LORD]] [[H430|his God]] [[H5414|delivered Ahaz]] [[H3027|into the hand]] [[H4428|of the king]] [[H758|of Aram,]] [[H5221|who attacked]] [[H7617|him and took]] [[H1419|many]] [[H7633|captives]] [[H1834|to Damascus.]] [[H1571|Ahaz was also]] [[H5414|delivered]] [[H3027|into the hand]] [[H4428|of the king]] [[H3478|of Israel,]] [[H5221|who struck]] [[H1419|him with great]] [[H4347|force.]] ^2805

[[H259|For in one]] [[H3117|day]] [[H6492|Pekah]] [[H1121|son]] [[H7425|of Remaliah]] [[H2026|killed]] [[H3967|120,000]] [[H2428|valiant]] [[H1121|men]] [[H3063|in Judah.]] ⟨This happened⟩ [[H5800|because they had forsaken]] [[H3068|the LORD,]] [[H430|the God]] [[H1|of their fathers.]] ^2806

[[H2147|Zichri,]] [[H669|an Ephraimite]] [[H1368|warrior,]] [[H2026|killed]] [[H4641|Maaseiah]] [[H1121|the son]] [[H4428|of the king,]] [[H5840|Azrikam]] [[H5057|the governor]] [[H1004|of the palace,]] [[H511|and Elkanah]] [[H4932|the second]] [[H4428|to the king.]] ^2807

[[H1121|Then the Israelites]] [[H3967|took 200,000]] [[H7617|captives]] [[H251|from their kinsmen—]] [[H802|women,]] [[H1121|sons,]] [[H1323|and daughters.]] [[H1571|They also]] [[H962|carried off]] [[H7227|a great deal of]] [[H7998|plunder]] [[H935|and brought]] [[H7998|it]] [[H8111|to Samaria.]] ^2808

[[H5030|But a prophet]] [[H3068|of the LORD]] [[H8034|named]] [[H5752|Oded]] [[H1961|was]] [[H8033|there,]] [[H3318|and he went out]] [[H6440|to meet]] [[H6635|the army]] [[H935|that returned]] [[H8111|to Samaria.]] [[H2009|“Look,”]] [[H559|he said]] [[H2534|to them,  “because of His wrath]] [[H5921|against]] [[H3063|Judah,]] [[H3068|the LORD,]] [[H430|the God]] [[H1|of your fathers,]] [[H5414|has delivered them]] [[H3027|into your hands.]] [[H2026|But you have slaughtered]] [[H2197|them  in a rage]] ⟨that⟩ [[H5060|reaches up]] [[H8064|to heaven.]] ^2809

[[H6258|And now]] [[H859|you]] [[H559|intend]] [[H3533|to reduce to slavery]] [[H5650|the men]] [[H8198|and women]] [[H3063|of Judah]] [[H3389|and Jerusalem.]] [[H859|But are you]] [[H3808|not]] [[H7535|also]] [[H819|guilty]] [[H3068|before the LORD]] [[H430|your God?]] ^2810

[[H6258|Now therefore,]] [[H8085|listen to me]] [[H7725|and return]] [[H7633|the captives]] [[H7617|you took]] [[H251|from your kinsmen,]] [[H3588|for]] [[H2740|the fierce anger]] [[H3069|of the LORD]] [[H5921|is upon you.”]] ^2811

[[H376|Then some]] [[H7218|of the leaders]] [[H1121|of the Ephraimites—]] [[H5838|Azariah]] [[H1121|son]] [[H3076|of Jehohanan,]] [[H1296|Berechiah]] [[H1121|son]] [[H4919|of Meshillemoth,]] [[H3169|Jehizkiah]] [[H1121|son]] [[H7967|of Shallum,]] [[H6021|and Amasa]] [[H1121|son]] [[H2311|of Hadlai—]] [[H6965|stood]] [[H5921|in opposition to]] [[H935|those arriving]] [[H4480|from]] [[H6635|the war.]] ^2812

[[H3808|“You must not]] [[H935|bring]] [[H7633|the captives]] [[H2008|here,”]] [[H559|they said,]] [[H3588|“for]] [[H859|you]] [[H559|are proposing]] [[H819|to bring guilt]] [[H5921|upon us]] [[H3068|from the LORD]] [[H3254|and to add]] [[H5921|to]] [[H2403|our sins]] [[H819|and our guilt.]] [[H3588|For]] [[H819|our  guilt]] [[H7227|is great,]] [[H2740|and fierce anger]] [[H5921|is upon]] [[H3478|Israel.”]] ^2813

[[H2502|So the armed men]] [[H5800|left]] [[H7633|the captives]] [[H961|and the plunder]] [[H6440|before]] [[H8269|the leaders]] [[H3605|and all]] [[H6951|the assembly.]] ^2814

[[H376|Then the men]] [[H834|who]] [[H5344|were designated]] [[H8034|by name]] [[H6965|arose,]] [[H2388|took charge]] [[H7633|of the captives,]] [[H4480|and provided from]] [[H7998|the plunder]] [[H3847|clothing]] [[H4636|for the naked.]] [[H3847|They clothed them,]] [[H5274|gave them sandals]] [[H398|and food]] [[H8248|and drink,]] [[H5480|anointed]] ⟨their wounds⟩, [[H5095|and put]] [[H3605|all]] [[H3782|the feeble]] [[H2543|on donkeys.]] [[H935|So they brought them]] [[H3405|to Jericho,]] [[H5892|the City]] [[H8558|of Palms,]] [[H681|to]] [[H251|their brothers.]] [[H7725|Then they returned]] [[H8111|to Samaria.]] ^2815

[[H1931|At that]] [[H6256|time]] [[H4428|King]] [[H271|Ahaz]] [[H7971|sent]] [[H5826|for help]] [[H5921|from]] [[H4428|the king]] [[H804|of Assyria.]] ^2816

[[H130|The Edomites]] [[H5750|had again]] [[H935|come]] [[H5221|and attacked]] [[H3063|Judah]] [[H7617|and carried away]] [[H7628|captives.]] ^2817

[[H3588|Although]] [[H271|Ahaz]] [[H2505|had taken a portion]] [[H1004|from the house]] [[H3068|of the LORD,]] [[H853|from]] [[H4428|the royal]] [[H1004|palace,]] [[H8269|and from the princes]] [[H5414|and had presented]] ⟨it⟩ [[H4428|to the king]] [[H804|of Assyria,]] [[H3808|it did not]] [[H5833|help him.]] ^2821

[[H6256|In the time]] [[H6887|of his distress,]] [[H4428|King]] [[H271|Ahaz]] [[H3254|became even more]] [[H4603|unfaithful]] [[H3068|to the LORD.]] ^2822

[[H6213|He made]] [[H5178|a bronze]] [[H4196|altar]] [[H6242|twenty]] [[H520|cubits]] [[H753|long,]] [[H6242|twenty]] [[H520|cubits]] [[H7341|wide,]] [[H6235|and ten]] [[H520|cubits]] [[H6967|high.]] ^0401

[[H2947|It was a handbreadth]] [[H5672|thick,]] [[H8193|and its rim]] [[H4639|was fashioned]] [[H8193|like the brim]] [[H3563|of a cup,]] [[H7799|like a lily]] [[H6525|blossom.]] [[H3557|It could hold]] [[H7969|three]] [[H505|thousand]] [[H1324|baths.]] ^0405

[[H935|When Micaiah arrived,]] [[H4428|the king]] [[H559|asked]] [[H413|him,]] [[H4318|“Micaiah,]] [[H1980|should we go]] [[H4421|to war]] [[H413|against]] [[H7433|Ramoth-gilead,]] [[H518|or]] [[H2308|should we refrain?”]] [[H5927|“Go up]] [[H6743|and triumph,”]] [[H559|Micaiah replied,]] [[H5414|“for they will be given]] [[H3027|into your hand.”]] ^1814

[[H3188|The genealogy]] [[H3605|included all]] [[H2945|the little ones,]] [[H802|wives,]] [[H1121|sons,]] [[H1323|and daughters]] [[H3605|in the whole]] [[H6951|assembly.]] [[H3588|For]] [[H530|they had faithfully]] [[H6942|consecrated themselves]] [[H6944|as holy.]] ^3118

[[H3548|As for the priests,]] [[H1121|the descendants]] [[H175|of Aaron,]] ⟨who lived on⟩ [[H7704|the farmlands]] [[H5892|around their cities,]] [[H3605|in each]] [[H5892|and every city,]] [[H376|men]] [[H5344|were designated]] [[H8034|by name]] [[H5414|to distribute]] [[H4490|a portion]] [[H3605|to every]] [[H2145|male]] [[H3548|among the priests]] [[H3605|and to every]] [[H3881|Levite]] [[H3187|listed by the genealogies.]] ^3119

[[H2063|So this is what]] [[H2396|Hezekiah]] [[H6213|did]] [[H3605|throughout]] [[H3063|Judah.]] [[H6213|He did]] [[H2896|what was good]] [[H3477|and upright]] [[H571|and true]] [[H6440|before]] [[H3068|the LORD]] [[H430|his God.]] ^3120

[[H558|Amaziah]] [[H6242|was twenty-five]] [[H1121|years old]] ⟨when⟩ [[H4427|he became king,]] [[H4427|and he reigned]] [[H3389|in Jerusalem]] [[H6242|twenty-nine]] [[H8141|years.]] [[H517|His mother’s]] [[H8034|name]] [[H3086|was Jehoaddan;]] [[H3389|she was from Jerusalem.]] ^2501

[[H558|Then Amaziah]] [[H6908|gathered]] ⟨the people of⟩ [[H3063|Judah]] [[H1|and assigned them according to their families]] [[H8269|to commanders]] [[H505|of thousands]] ⟨and⟩ [[H8269|]] [[H3967|of hundreds.]] [[H6485|And he numbered]] [[H6242|those twenty]] [[H1121|years of age]] [[H4605|or older]] [[H3605|throughout]] [[H3063|Judah]] [[H1144|and Benjamin]] [[H4672|and found]] [[H7969|there to be 300,000]] [[H970|choice]] ⟨men⟩, ⟨able⟩ [[H3318|to serve]] [[H6635|in the army,]] [[H270|bearing]] [[H7420|the spear]] [[H6793|and shield.]] ^2505

[[H376|But a man]] [[H430|of God]] [[H935|came]] [[H413|to him]] [[H559|and said,]] [[H4428|“O king,]] [[H408|do not let]] [[H6635|the army]] [[H3478|of Israel]] [[H935|go]] [[H5973|with you,]] [[H3588|for]] [[H3069|the LORD]] [[H369|is not]] [[H5973|with]] [[H3478|Israel—]] ⟨not with⟩ [[H3605|any]] [[H1121|of the Ephraimites.]] ^2507

[[H2005|If]] [[H6113|I close]] [[H8064|the sky]] [[H1961|so there is]] [[H3808|no]] [[H4306|rain,]] [[H2005|or if]] [[H6680|I command]] [[H2284|the locust]] [[H398|to devour]] [[H776|the land,]] [[H518|or if]] [[H7971|I send]] [[H1698|a plague]] [[H5971|among My people,]] ^0713

[[H5971|and My people]] [[H834|who]] [[H7121|are called]] [[H5921|by]] [[H8034|My name]] [[H3665|humble themselves]] [[H6419|and pray]] [[H1245|and seek]] [[H6440|My face,]] [[H7725|and turn]] [[H4480|from]] [[H7451|their wicked]] [[H1870|ways,]] [[H589|then I]] [[H8085|will hear]] [[H8064|from heaven,]] [[H5545|forgive]] [[H2403|their sin,]] [[H7495|and heal]] [[H776|their land.]] ^0714

[[H6258|Now]] [[H5869|My eyes]] [[H1961|will be]] [[H6605|open]] [[H241|and My ears]] [[H7183|attentive]] [[H8605|to the prayers offered]] [[H2088|in this]] [[H4725|place.]] ^0715

[[H977|For I have now chosen]] [[H6942|and consecrated]] [[H2088|this]] [[H1004|house]] [[H8034|so that My Name]] [[H1961|may be]] [[H8033|there]] [[H5704|forever.]] [[H5869|My eyes]] [[H3820|and My heart]] [[H1961|will be]] [[H8033|there]] [[H3605|for all time.]] ^0716

[[H859|And as for you,]] [[H518|if]] [[H1980|you walk]] [[H6440|before]] [[H834|Me as]] [[H1|your father]] [[H1732|David]] [[H1980|walked,]] [[H6213|doing]] [[H3605|all]] [[H6680|I have commanded you,]] [[H8104|and if you keep]] [[H2706|My statutes]] [[H4941|and ordinances,]] ^0717

[[H6965|then I will establish]] [[H4438|your royal]] [[H3678|throne,]] [[H834|as]] [[H3772|I covenanted]] [[H1|with your father]] [[H1732|David]] [[H559|when I said,]] [[H3808|‘You will never]] [[H3772|fail]] [[H376|to have a man]] [[H4910|to rule]] [[H3478|over Israel.’]] ^0718

[[H518|But if]] [[H859|you]] [[H7725|turn away]] [[H5800|and forsake]] [[H2708|the statutes]] [[H4687|and the commandments]] [[H5414|I have set]] [[H6440|before you,]] [[H1980|and if you go off]] [[H5647|to serve]] [[H7812|and worship]] [[H312|other]] [[H430|gods,]] ^0719

[[H5428|then I will uproot Israel]] [[H5921|from]] [[H127|the soil]] [[H5414|I have given]] [[H2088|them,  and this]] [[H1004|temple]] [[H834|that]] [[H6942|I have sanctified]] [[H8034|for My Name]] [[H7993|I will banish]] [[H5921|from]] [[H6440|My presence.]] [[H5414|I will make it]] [[H4912|an object of scorn]] [[H8148|and ridicule]] [[H3605|among all]] [[H5971|the peoples.]] ^0720

[[H2088|And this]] [[H1004|temple]] [[H1961|will now]] [[H5945|become a heap of rubble.]] [[H3605|All]] [[H5674|who pass]] [[H5921|it by]] [[H8074|will be appalled]] [[H559|and say,]] [[H4100|‘Why]] [[H3068|has the LORD]] [[H6213|done]] [[H3602|such a thing]] [[H2063|to this]] [[H776|land]] [[H2088|and to this]] [[H1004|temple?’]] ^0721

[[H559|And will answer,]] ⟨others⟩ [[H5921|‘Because]] [[H5800|they have forsaken]] [[H3068|the LORD,]] [[H430|the God]] [[H1|of their fathers,]] [[H834|who]] [[H3318|brought them out]] [[H4714|of Egypt,]] [[H2388|and have embraced]] [[H312|other]] [[H430|gods,]] [[H7812|worshiping]] [[H5647|and serving them.]] [[H5921|Because of]] [[H3651|this,]] [[H935|He has brought]] [[H3605|all]] [[H2063|this]] [[H7451|disaster]] [[H5921|upon them.]] ^0722

[[H8010|Then Solomon]] [[H2490|began]] [[H1129|to build]] [[H1004|the house]] [[H3069|of the LORD]] [[H3389|in Jerusalem]] [[H2022|on Mount]] [[H4179|Moriah,]] [[H834|where]] ⟨the LORD⟩ [[H7200|had appeared]] [[H1|to his father]] [[H1732|David.]] ⟨This was⟩ [[H4725|the place that]] [[H1732|David]] [[H3559|had prepared]] [[H1637|on the threshing floor]] [[H771|of Ornan]] [[H2983|the Jebusite.]] ^0301

⟨Solomon⟩ [[H2490|began]] [[H1129|construction]] [[H8145|on the second]] [[H8145|day of the second]] [[H2320|month]] [[H702|in the fourth]] [[H8141|year]] [[H4438|of his reign.]] ^0302

[[H3245|The foundation]] [[H8010|that Solomon]] [[H1129|laid]] [[H1004|for the house]] [[H430|of God]] ⟨was⟩ [[H8346|sixty]] [[H520|cubits]] [[H753|long]] [[H6242|and twenty]] [[H520|cubits]] [[H7341|wide,]] [[H7223|according to the old]] [[H4060|standard.]] ^0303

[[H197|The portico]] [[H5921|at]] [[H6440|the front,]] [[H5921|extending across]] [[H7341|the width]] [[H1004|of the temple,]] ⟨was⟩ [[H6242|twenty]] [[H520|cubits]] ⟨long⟩ ⟨and⟩ [[H3967|]] [[H6242|twenty]] ⟨cubits⟩ [[H1363|high.]] [[H6823|He overlaid]] [[H6441|the inside]] [[H2889|with pure]] [[H2091|gold.]] ^0304

[[H2645|He paneled]] [[H1419|the main]] [[H1004|room]] [[H6086|with]] [[H1265|cypress,]] [[H2645|which he overlaid]] [[H2896|with fine]] [[H2091|gold]] [[H5927|and decorated]] [[H8561|with palm tree]] [[H8333|and chain]] ⟨designs⟩. ^0305

[[H6823|He adorned]] [[H1004|the temple]] [[H3368|with precious]] [[H68|stones]] [[H8597|for beauty,]] [[H2091|and its gold]] ⟨was⟩ [[H2091|]] [[H6516|from Parvaim.]] ^0306

[[H2645|He overlaid]] ⟨its⟩ [[H1004|]] [[H6982|beams,]] [[H5592|thresholds,]] [[H7023|walls,]] [[H1817|and doors]] [[H2091|with gold,]] [[H6605|and he carved]] [[H3742|cherubim]] [[H5921|on]] [[H7023|the walls.]] ^0307

[[H6213|Then he made]] [[H6944|the Most Holy]] [[H1004|Place;]] [[H753|its length]] [[H5921|corresponded to]] [[H7341|the width]] [[H1004|of the temple,]] [[H6242|twenty]] [[H520|cubits]] ⟨long⟩ [[H6242|and twenty]] [[H520|cubits]] [[H7341|wide,]] [[H2645|and he overlaid]] ⟨the inside⟩ [[H8337|with six]] [[H3967|hundred]] [[H3603|talents]] [[H2896|of fine]] [[H2091|gold.]] ^0308

[[H4948|The weight]] [[H4548|of the nails]] [[H2572|was fifty]] [[H8255|shekels]] [[H2091|of gold.]] [[H2645|He also overlaid]] [[H5944|the upper area]] [[H2091|with gold.]] ^0309

[[H6944|In the Most Holy]] [[H1004|Place]] [[H6213|he made]] [[H8147|two]] [[H3742|cherubim]] [[H6816|of sculptured]] [[H4639|work,]] [[H6823|and he overlaid]] [[H2091|them with gold.]] ^0310

[[H753|The total]] [[H3671|wingspan]] [[H3742|of the cherubim]] ⟨was⟩ [[H6242|twenty]] [[H520|cubits.]] [[H3671|One wing]] [[H259|of the first]] ⟨cherub⟩ ⟨was⟩ [[H2568|five]] [[H520|cubits]] ⟨long⟩ [[H5060|and touched]] [[H7023|the wall]] [[H1004|of the temple,]] [[H312|and other]] ⟨its⟩ [[H3671|wing]] ⟨was⟩ [[H2568|five]] [[H520|cubits]] ⟨long⟩ [[H5060|and touched]] [[H3671|the wing]] [[H312|of the other]] [[H3742|cherub.]] ^0311

[[H3671|The wing]] [[H259|of the second]] [[H3742|cherub]] ⟨also measured⟩ [[H2568|five]] [[H520|cubits]] [[H5060|and touched]] [[H7023|the wall]] [[H1004|of the house,]] [[H312|while other]] ⟨its⟩ [[H3671|wing]] ⟨measured⟩ [[H2568|five]] [[H520|cubits]] [[H1695|and touched]] [[H3671|the wing]] [[H312|of the first]] [[H3742|cherub.]] ^0312

[[H3671|So the total wingspan]] [[H428|of these]] [[H3742|cherubim]] ⟨was⟩ [[H6242|twenty]] [[H520|cubits.]] [[H1992|They]] [[H5975|stood]] [[H5921|on]] [[H7272|their feet,]] [[H6440|facing]] [[H1004|the room.]] ⟨main⟩ ^0313

[[H6213|He made]] [[H6532|the veil]] [[H8504|of blue,]] [[H713|purple,]] [[H3758|and crimson yarn]] [[H948|and fine linen,]] [[H3742|with cherubim]] [[H5927|woven]] [[H5921|into it.]] ^0314

[[H6440|In front]] [[H1004|of the temple]] [[H6213|he made]] [[H8147|two]] [[H5982|pillars,]] [[H7970|which were thirty-five]] ⟨together⟩ [[H520|cubits]] [[H753|high,]] [[H6858|each with a capital]] [[H5921|on]] [[H7218|top]] ⟨measuring⟩ [[H2568|five]] [[H520|cubits.]] ^0315

[[H6965|Then he set up]] [[H5982|the pillars]] [[H5921|in]] [[H6440|front]] [[H1964|of the temple,]] [[H259|one]] [[H3225|on the south]] [[H259|and one]] [[H8040|on the north.]] ⟨The pillar⟩ [[H3227|on the south]] [[H7121|he named]] [[H3199|Jachin,]] [[H8042|and the on the north]] ⟨pillar⟩ [[H8034|he named]] [[H1162|Boaz.]] ^0317
